<GmapID>0x80dc732bc40d1c17:0xea9cd95428e322d6< /GmapID><name>Chris J</name><userid>113759434297879406228<//userid>< review>
While most of the post about the carts were valid the blame was made on a company that has nothing to do with parking lot it resides in. Many parking lots are privately and separately owned by a business. Yes the parking lot does not have many cart drop-off" locations, but the problems are on the customers, and the parking lot owner, not Ralph's. The owner has hired a guard to help with the rule breakers (it's privately owned, that's why there is no smoking in the food court, get over it you smokers)

I have found that the people in that particular area of Carlsbad make no attempt to place the carts near or in the cart areas. The locals enjoy placing them right next to your vehicle so it can be damaged. They don't even find an empty space, I watched a man driving a nice BMW slam his cart in to mine, and left his trash in the cart and even on the ground. All the customers care about is themselves. The parking lot consists of one way lanes yet the customers go the wrong way, and speed. Yes the locals speed like mad, blow through the stops (clearly marked on the ground), nearly hit a few people, only to get a cup of coffee at Starbucks. The sad thing is that these "wrong doers" are adults. NOT KIDS, they are aged from 30+ and have an air of self entitlement. I avoid the  store just because of the customers.

Now about the store. The store is absolutely beautiful. The prices are a little high, yes, but we are in Carlsbad, not Chula Vista. The staff was nice, and the cashier, treated my son and I wonderfully (maybe because we had the same name?) THE BATHROOMS WERE EMMACULATE!!! I didn't feel like I had the risk of getting some STD's just while using them! It's a shame i have to give it 4 stars. It's all due to the citizens of Carlsbad.< /review>

Great Customer Service & Products

I am always greeted with a smile and an employee always makes it a point to offer assistance within 30 seconds of me walking in the store., without being too "pushy".
The employees are very knowledgably about the available products and are quick to detail all the cool new features.
After deciding to purchase an item the employees will offer to engrave the product, if available, and detail the services offered for cleaning and repairing at little to no cost.
I have purchased fossil watches, purses and wallets over the years and every single item is in impeccable condition. I highly recommend this store and Fossil watches, purses and wallets.</review>

< name>
William Bryson</name>
< date>
1511574425276</date>
<Gmap_id>0x808fbc4687f9488b:0xedc9d2633732b534< /Gmap_id>< Review>
Beautiful place to go in the evenings. Great views across the bay towards Palo Alto. The sun sets behind the bridge from the pier. Access is free as is parking. About 200 meters from the start of the pier is a large passage that allows access to the other side of hwy 84 giving you views across the bay towards San Francisco. From there you see the the sunset behind the coastal hills.
Go on one of the mixed clouds and sky days after the rain in the winter for spectacular sunset‚Äôs.
From this point you could walk almost to Berkeley along the salt pond levies.
Many coastal dwelling birds for the bird watchers.
At the beginning of the road to the pier are wonderful marshy areas you can explore. All in all a hidden gem in our neighborhood. NOTE:  never go in the exit lane if you get there late. SEVERE TIRE DAMAGE from one way spikes in the road.</Review>

We got our Goldendoodle through PuppySpot after searching local breeders that had 6-12 mos waiting lists. PuppySpot was great, Because we could search the size and color and generation that we were looking for easily on the app. We had the puppy we wanted within a matter of weeks, Instead of placing a deposit and wondering if the puppy that you want will be available in six months to a year. He is the perfect addition to our family! Very happy and healthy! The cons of going through puppy spot is that you pay more for the convenience, and they could definitely improve on some of the communication during the waiting process. <name>James Welsh< /name><Date>1585340360027< /Date>< rating>
5</rating>
< Text>
Puppyspot is an incredible company of employees who genuinely care about the dogs. I found my dog on their site last year and I am looking to get another one right now. I've been searching for a good company for forever and I'm glad that I've finally found the one. I must admit, some of the reviews made me question Puppyspot, but after going through the process and actually taking the time to understand the company, I can testify that anything under five stars is a lie. The biggest trend on some of the negative reviews is that the dog had a small health problem or that the prices were too high. Mine did not have a health problem, but even if he did, it wouldn't be a big deal. I hate to break it to you, but dogs (like humans) sometimes get sick. Puppyspot takes their dogs' health extremely seriously and requires all dogs to receive a veterinarian check before they leave the breeder.  Plus, if there are any major health problems, the company pays for all the medical care. The people at Puppyspot love these dogs and the Puppy concierge who spoke to me told me that Puppyspot would take the dog and re-home him if I wasn't able to support him. I got the vibe that Puppyspot doesn't play games when it comes to the health of their puppies. In fact, in speaking with the concierge, I learned that the Puppyspot team actually examines individuals who want to buy their puppies to ensure that they are responsible owners. In short, they do not let just anyone receive a puppy, just like they deny 90% of all breeders who attempt to join Puppyspot and don't meet their high standard. The second major complaint (which I realised was a bit dumb) was that the prices were too high. Yes, Puppyspot does have some expensive dogs, but that is because they do not sacrifice on quality. What sold me, was that you are paying for the trust. I was able to trust that Puppyspot vetted all the breeders (Puppyspot denies 90% of the breeders who apply and has dedicated teams to drive all across the country and inspect breeders) and trust that all safety precautions were taken. <Text>I want to make this as detailed as possible to hopefully alleviate some of the fear and anxiety that I experienced for anyone who decides to go ahead with this company. I read a bunch of reviews on Google, Yelp, Puppyspot and BBB that were a mix bag, but those bad reviews were what I focused on, unfortunately, while I waited for my puppy to arrive. I wish I would have had more faith that everything would work out...because it absolutely did!

It took me 8 years to be ready to adopt another Pomeranian. I lost my little Rylie and he was my first baby, my first dog, my first "child," so it was a great loss that took time to get over. When I first started looking, I checked breeders in the area. Most the puppies were either adopted right away, or you had to put a deposit down for a dog that you couldn't even tell what it was going to look like and these pups were a minimum of $1500 each for that breed. Because of the fore mentioned issues and upfront cost, going through someone locally was out of the question for me. I did a lot of researching of PuppySpot prior to deciding to adopt from them. I looked for the right puppy for weeks then found my little "Lane." He was the perfect looking, the right price and I was even able to finance him, without that option I wouldn't have been able to get a Pomeranian at all. I do realize the cost is much more expensive than going elsewhere, but I, like all their other customers, know that going in and I don't understand why anyone would complain after they committed to paying the, yes inflated, but fully disclosed cost of their new puppy. I put my $99.00 deposit down and signed the contract. I am billed by checking account draft, bi-weekly on my paydays.

I was expecting for my puppy to arrive 9 days later on a Wednesday. After 2 days, I was told the option of flying in my puppy to Phoenix was no longer available due to a "heat embargo" and he would have to fly in to Flagstaff (4 hours each way). I told them that was not an option and I could not travel that far to pick up the puppy. They then called me back and told me it would just be another $200 and they could send him ground transportation to have him there a week later, arriving between Tuesday and Thursday. I got angry at that point and told them that I am not committing one more dime to getting this dog (I already rolled in $399 to my financing to fly him in) and they can cancel my account if that's the only option. They then put a Manager on and he calmed me down and told me they would take care of the ground cost. I agreed.

They let me know to download the PuppySpot app that you can converse with your Puppy Manager, see pics of your puppy and see the info about the pups parents, etc. I requested pictures that I received within 72 hours and thought that he looked a little sickly in them, so I requested a video to see him that he was in fact active and healthy, which I got a day later. The videos put my mind at ease. He was spunky and apparently happy and well taken care of by the breeder. It was obvious he lived inside in a warm, clean, loving environment.  My arrival date did get pushed back to Friday, but that wasn't a big deal. They always responded to my questions within a couple hours, if not right away, and I was super high maintenance with a bad attitude and a lot of mistrust, paranoia from continually reading the bad reviews, freaking my self out.

When the transport company picked him up, they sent a pic to let me know they had him. I was able to text the transport company and check on the baby during the 5 day trip.

When he arrived, he was smaller than I had anticipated from the pictures (3 lbs) and about ten times as cute! The two puppies have been playing for 4 hours straight and his temperament is so sweet and playful. He is a gorgeous, perfect little guy and everything went wonderfully, no matter my reservations.

<Review>It's got the air of a hole in the wall restaurant from the outside, but do not judge them by the exterior. it really does have the best Mediterranean food in the area. They have a vegetarian plate which is really just the sides grouped together as a single plate, so my vegetarian friends weren't overly impressed, but I love the lule, the kabobs, and the sides are super flavorful even if not filling by themselves. The salmon also got high marks from my friend. The prices are reasonable too.

It's in an industrial area where there aren't many comparable options nearby and the locals like this place so be prepared. If you get there at noon, you should get a table without too much trouble. Get there at 12:30 though and you might have to wait.</Review>< Pics>

A friend and I tried this little out-of-the way restaurant for dinner, mext to a marine repair shop. An add place for a restaurant, I thought. It was deserted the evening we went... not another customer in sight. Too bad, because the food was very good. <Text>Oddly situated restaurant in the middle of an industrial area in Burbank. You'd easily drive by this place without a second thought. The interior is relatively spare but seats more than you'd expect.

I ordered to go and the beef in the beef salad was still tender and juicy even after sitting in the to-go box for an hour. The ikra was one of the better ones I've had. I'm not sure why it's universally called eggplant caviar because there's no caviar nor eggs for that matter. The Armenian coffee was strong without a huge amount of sludge.

Parking is plentiful on the other side of the street with diagonal stalls set along the entire street.</Text>< Pics>

< review>
Great spot! It's my new go-to before or after a flight out of Burbank--the airport is literally a 3 minute drive.

The food is fantastic. A heaping plate of two pieces of flavorful lule kebab on rice plus two samplings of their appetizers (love the smoky eggplant dip and tzatziki-like yogurt dip) and pita will set you back $6.75. A sprinkling of sumac seals the deal.

The place is a local, family-owned restaurant with friendly and attentive waitstaff. They have beers on tap and apparently live music on Saturdays to keep things festive. Looking forward to returning again and again.<//review>

< rating>
4</rating>
< text>
Could have received the 5th star if there was more value in the meal. I bought the Chicken and Beef Shish combo plate and only got 4 pieces of beef when I should've been given 5.
Aside from missing that piece of beef I was also given maybe 2 spoonfuls of Tabule. You'd expect a fuller plate as the partition on the plate could've easily held at least 4 times the amount given. Especially when I look at some of the photos posted by other Yelpers, seems like they received a lot more than I did.

As far as the quality and taste of the food, I can't complain. Definitely delicious, but you could get so much more and just as good, if not better, at Zankou Chicken paying a few dollars less. I don't nickel and dime, but in terms of value (and a missing piece of beef) for a first timer, I had to rate this a 4 star.</text>
